This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The conversation is summarized below:
Analysis:
Let me chronologically analyze the conversation:

1. **Initial Request**: User reported a network timeout error (30000ms exceeded) when trying to access the application. Multiple API endpoints were failing with timeout errors.

2. **First Diagnosis**: I identified that the backend server was not running. The error logs showed multiple API calls timing out:
   - `/api/user/settings` (LanguageLoader)
   - `/api/menus` (MenuProvider)
   - `/api/menus/favorites`
   - `/api/menus/recent`
   - `/api/menus/by-path`
   - `/api/permissions` (PermissionProvider)

3. **First Solution**: I checked the package.json and found that the backend should run on port 3001. I verified the backend wasn't running and instructed the user to start it with `npm run dev` or `npm run dev:backend`.

4. **Second Request**: User reported that `http://localhost:3000/admin/user-role-mapping` page was not loading, showing the same timeout error specifically for `/api/role` endpoint.

5. **Second Diagnosis**: I analyzed the code and discovered an **N+1 query problem** in the `/api/user-role-mapping` endpoint when `includeDetails=true` parameter was used. The issue was:
   - The code was calling `enrichMappingWithDetails()` for each mapping individually
   - Each call made separate database queries for user and role information
   - For 100 mappings, this resulted in 201 database queries (1 + 100 + 100)
   - This caused the 30-second timeout

6. **Second Solution**: I optimized the code in `backend/routes/userRoleMapping.js`:
   - Changed from individual queries to batch loading
   - Load all users and roles once with `Promise.all()`
   - Created Map lookups for O(1) access
   - Reduced queries from 201 to 3
   - Expected performance improvement: 30+ seconds â†’ 1-2 seconds

7. **Implementation**: 
   - I killed the existing backend process (PID 27036)
   - Started the backend server again
   - Backend successfully started and connected to PostgreSQL database

8. **Third Request**: User reported that `http://localhost:3000/ko/admin/help` page is not working properly - program ID, language, and status values are not showing. This is the current pending task.

Key files examined:
- `backend/routes/role.js` - Role API routes
- `backend/services/roleService.js` - Role service layer
- `backend/routes/userRoleMapping.js` - User-role mapping routes (MODIFIED)
- `backend/services/userService.js` - User service (checked for getAllUsers method)
- `src/app/[locale]/admin/user-role-mapping/page.tsx` - Frontend page making the API calls

The conversation is in Korean, but the technical content and code are in English.

Summary:
1. **Primary Request and Intent:**
   - Initial: Diagnose and fix network timeout errors (30000ms) preventing the application from loading
   - Second: Fix timeout issue on user-role-mapping page (`http://localhost:3000/admin/user-role-mapping`)
   - Current: Fix the help page (`http://localhost:3000/ko/admin/help`) where program ID, language, and status values are not displaying

2. **Key Technical Concepts:**
   - **N+1 Query Problem**: Performance anti-pattern where database queries scale linearly with dataset size
   - **Batch Loading**: Loading all required data in a single query instead of multiple sequential queries
   - **Map-based Lookups**: Using JavaScript Map for O(1) constant-time data access
   - **Promise.all()**: Parallel execution of multiple async operations
   - **PostgreSQL Database**: Backend database storing users, roles, and mappings
   - **Express.js Backend**: Node.js server running on port 3001
   - **Next.js Frontend**: React application running on port 3000
   - **API Timeout Configuration**: 30-second timeout in axios configuration

3. **Files and Code Sections:**

   - **`backend/routes/userRoleMapping.js`** (MODIFIED)
     - **Why Important**: Contains the API endpoint causing timeout due to N+1 query problem
     - **Changes Made**: Optimized GET `/api/user-role-mapping` endpoint with `includeDetails=true` parameter
     - **Before (Slow approach)**:
     ```javascript
     // Enrich with user and role details if requested
     if (includeDetails === 'true') {
       const enrichedMappings = await Promise.all(
         mappings.map((m) => enrichMappingWithDetails(m))  // N+1 queries
       );
       return res.json({
         mappings: enrichedMappings,
         total: enrichedMappings.length
       });
     }
     ```
     - **After (Optimized approach)**:
     ```javascript
     // Enrich with user and role details if requested
     if (includeDetails === 'true') {
       // OPTIMIZED: Load all users and roles once to avoid N+1 queries
       const [allUsers, allRoles] = await Promise.all([
         userService.getAllUsers(),
         roleService.getAllRoles()
       ]);

       // Create lookup maps for O(1) access
       const userMap = new Map(allUsers.map(u => [u.id, u]));
       const roleMap = new Map(allRoles.map(r => [r.id, r]));

       const enrichedMappings = mappings.map(m => {
         const user = userMap.get(m.user_id);
         const role = roleMap.get(m.role_id);

         return {
           id: m.id,
           userId: m.user_id,
           roleId: m.role_id,
           assignedBy: m.assigned_by,
           assignedAt: m.assigned_at,
           expiresAt: m.expires_at,
           isActive: m.is_active,
           updatedAt: m.updated_at,
           updatedBy: m.updated_by,
           userName: user?.username || user?.name,
           userEmail: user?.email,
           userDepartment: user?.department,
           roleName: role?.name,
           roleDisplayName: role?.display_name
         };
       });

       return res.json({
         mappings: enrichedMappings,
         total: enrichedMappings.length
       });
     }
     ```

   - **`src/app/[locale]/admin/user-role-mapping/page.tsx`** (READ)
